class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sports_in_Florida" title="Sports in Florida">Sports in Florida</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg/220px-Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg/330px-Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg/440px-Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Daytona_International_Speedway_2011.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\n<a href="/wiki/Daytona_International_Speedway" title="Daytona International Speedway">Daytona International Speedway</a> is home to various auto racing events</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>Florida has three <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">NFL</a> teams, two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MLB" title="MLB">MLB</a> teams, two <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">NBA</a> teams, two <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">NHL</a> teams, and one <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MLS" title="MLS">MLS</a> team. Florida gained its first permanent major-league professional sports team in 1966 when the <a href="/wiki/American_Football_League" title="American Football League">American Football League</a> added the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Dolphins" title="Miami Dolphins">Miami Dolphins</a>. The state of Florida has given professional sports franchises some subsidies in the form of tax breaks since 1991.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-240"><a href="#cite_note-240">[240]</a></sup></p>\n<p>About half of all <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> teams conduct <a href="/wiki/Spring_training" title="Spring training">spring training</a> in the state, with teams informally organized into the "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grapefruit_League" title="Grapefruit League">Grapefruit League</a>". Throughout MLB history, other teams have held spring training in Florida.</p>\n<p><a href="/wiki/NASCAR" title="NASCAR">NASCAR</a> (headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Daytona_Beach,_Florida" title="Daytona Beach, Florida">Daytona Beach</a>) begins all three of its major auto racing series in Florida at <a href="/wiki/Daytona_International_Speedway" title="Daytona International Speedway">Daytona International Speedway</a> in February, featuring the <a href="/wiki/Daytona_500" title="Daytona 500">Daytona 500</a>, and ends all three Series in November at <a href="/wiki/Homestead-Miami_Speedway" title="Homestead-Miami Speedway">Homestead-Miami Speedway</a>. Daytona also has the <a href="/wiki/Coke_Zero_400" title="Coke Zero 400">Coke Zero 400</a> NASCAR race weekend around <a href="/wiki/Independence_Day_(United_States)" title="Independence Day (United States)">Independence Day</a> in July. The <a href="/wiki/24_Hours_of_Daytona" title="24 Hours of Daytona">24 Hours of Daytona</a> is one of the world\'s most prestigious endurance auto races. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_of_St._Petersburg" title="Grand Prix of St. Petersburg">Grand Prix of St. Petersburg</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_of_Miami_(Indycar)" title="Grand Prix of Miami (Indycar)">Grand Prix of Miami</a> have held <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/IndyCar" title="IndyCar">IndyCar</a> races as well.</p>\n<p>Florida is a major golf hub. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Professional_Golfers_Association_of_America" title="Professional Golfers Association of America">PGA of America</a> is headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_Gardens,_Florida" title="Palm Beach Gardens, Florida">Palm Beach Gardens</a>, the <a href="/wiki/PGA_Tour" title="PGA Tour">PGA Tour</a> is headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Ponte_Vedra_Beach,_Florida" title="Ponte Vedra Beach, Florida">Ponte Vedra Beach</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/LPGA" title="LPGA">LPGA</a> is headquartered in Daytona Beach. <a href="/wiki/The_Players_Championship" title="The Players Championship">The Players Championship</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WGC-Cadillac_Championship" title="WGC-Cadillac Championship">WGC-Cadillac Championship</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arnold_Palmer_Invitational" title="Arnold Palmer Invitational">Arnold Palmer Invitational</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honda_Classic" title="Honda Classic">Honda Classic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Valspar_Championship" title="Valspar Championship">Valspar Championship</a> are <a href="/wiki/PGA_Tour" title="PGA Tour">PGA Tour</a> rounds.</p>\n<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miami_Masters" title="Miami Masters">Miami Masters</a> is an <a href="/wiki/ATP_World_Tour_Masters_1000" title="ATP World Tour Masters 1000">ATP World Tour Masters 1000</a> and <a href="/wiki/WTA_Premier_tournaments" title="WTA Premier tournaments">WTA Premier</a> tennis event, whereas the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delray_Beach_International_Tennis_Championships" title="Delray Beach International Tennis Championships">Delray Beach International Tennis Championships</a> is an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ATP_World_Tour_250" title="ATP World Tour 250">ATP World Tour 250</a> event.</p>\n<p>Minor league baseball, <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">football</a>, basketball, <a href="/wiki/Ice_hockey" title="Ice hockey">ice hockey</a>, soccer and <a href="/wiki/Indoor_American_football" title="Indoor American football">indoor football</a> teams are based in Florida. Three of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arena_Football_League_(2010)" title="Arena Football League (2010)">Arena Football League</a>\'s teams are in Florida.</p>\n<p>Florida\'s universities have a number of <a href="/wiki/National_Collegiate_Athletic_Association" title="National Collegiate Athletic Association">collegiate sport</a> programs, especially the <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_Seminoles" title="Florida State Seminoles">Florida State Seminoles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miami_Hurricanes" title="Miami Hurricanes">Miami Hurricanes</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Coast_Conference" title="Atlantic Coast Conference">Atlantic Coast Conference</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Florida_Gators" title="Florida Gators">Florida Gators</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Southeastern_Conference" title="Southeastern Conference">Southeastern Conference</a>.</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable">\n<caption>Florida major league professional sports
